! ============ !
! Proper nouns !
! ============ !

! Note: the final non-sámi consonants: 
!          b  d  g  h  m  n  p  z
! write as b3 d3 g3 h3 m3 n3 p3 z3

! j that shall always be j (also in V_C) is written j3, as eg. in Ajja (Aj3ja) 

! Table of content
! ----------------
! Continuation lexica
! Personal names
!  First names
!  Surnames
! Place names
! ----------------

! Aspell lexica
! =============

! This is a lexicon to be used with aspell spell checker only.
! Target is to use as many sublexicons as possible with as many variables 
! as possible to create aspell affix file.

LEXICON AspellProp
Aspell LONDON ;
Spelle ACCRA ;
! DEATNU & MARJA use same affixes as GOAHTI
Cbern:Cbern3 BERN ;		! Same as BLIND
Duominen:Duomi C-FI-NEN ;
Blondon:Blondon3 LONDON ;		! VUOLAB goes here
Enystø NYSTØ ;
! PLACE-DIM is same as DIMINC
Ejeakkit:Ejeaggi ALEUHTAT ;



! Continuation lexica
! ===================

! Some of the entries point to continuation lexica in the sme-lex.txt
! file, such as GOAHTI. This implies that names have the same inflection as
! ordinary nouns, which is probably not true. These lexica must thus be re-
! vised as soon as the lexica for names become more accurate.

! Continuation lexica for personal names
! --------------------------------------

! Vowel final names
! - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON ACCRA-obj
 ACCRA ; 
LEXICON ACCRA-org
 ACCRA ; 
LEXICON ACCRA-mal
 ACCRA ; 
LEXICON ACCRA-fem
 ACCRA ; 
LEXICON ACCRA-sur
 ACCRA ;
LEXICON ACCRA-plc ! Place names
 ACCRA ;

LEXICON ACCRA ! Vowel-final names without Gradation and Ill change
! These sublexica are irrelevant for ACCRA, but added
! for the sake of the lexicon MARJA
 ACCRA-DC ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@ ACCRA-I ;		! correct suffixes
 @U.Cap.Obl@ ACCRA-OBL ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@ ACCRA-IICASE ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@ DenominalAdjsC ; !^C^

LEXICON GIEDDI ! Vowel final names with Gradation and Comp. forms
 @U.Cap.Obl@ GIEDDI-OBL ;
 @U.Cap.Opt@ GIEDDI-DC ; !^C^

LEXICON GIEDDI-OBL
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:n K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:X3j K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:X4 K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:X4 K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:X4s K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:X4t K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:X5 K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:X5jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:X5jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:X5jde K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:X5jn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:X5jgujn K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom:X6 K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom:X8 K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Sg+Nom:X4b K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Attr:X4b K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Sg+Gen:X4bu K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Sg+Gen:X4b K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Sg+Acc:X4bu K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Sg+Acc:X4b K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Sg+Ill:X4buj K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Sg+Loc:X4bus K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Sg+Com:X4bujn K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Pl+Nom:X4but K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Pl+Gen:X4bujd K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Pl+Acc:X4bujd K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Pl+Ill:X4bujdda K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Pl+Loc:X4bujn K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Pl+Com:X4bujgujn K ;
 +N+Prop+Comp+Ess:X4bun K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Attr:X4muss K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Sg+Nom:X4muss K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Sg+Nom:X4muss R ; !^C^
 +N+Prop+Superl+Sg+Gen:X4musa K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Sg+Acc:X4musa K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Sg+Ill:X4mussij K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Sg+Loc:X4musas K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Sg+Com:X4musajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Pl+Nom:X4musat K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Pl+Gen:X4musajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Pl+Acc:X4musajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Pl+Ill:X4musaide K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Pl+Loc:X4musajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Pl+Com:X4musajgujn K ;
 +N+Prop+Superl+Ess:X4mussan K ;
 +N+Prop+š+Dimin:X8ž PLACE-DIM-DECL ;
 +N+Prop: DenominalNounsV ;				!^C^

LEXICON GIEDDI-DC						!^C^
 +N+Prop: DenominalAdjsV ;				!^C^

LEXICON ROMSA-plc
ROMSA ;

 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:Y6jn K ;

LEXICON DEATNU ! Vowel final names with Gradation and Ill change (place names)
MARJA ;
! The separate lexicon was kept in case we need separate treatment
! of place and person in the future. Most MARJA entries are personal names, 
! and all DEATNU entries are placenames.


LEXICON MARJA-org
MARJA ;

LEXICON MARJA-mal
MARJA ;

LEXICON MARJA-sur
MARJA ;

LEXICON MARJA-fem
MARJA ;

LEXICON MARJA-plc
MARJA ;


LEXICON MARJA ! Vowel-final names with Gradation and Ill change (person names)
 ACCRA-DC ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@:@U.Cap.Obl@X3 ACCRA-I ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@:@U.Cap.Obl@X4 ACCRA-OBL ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@:@U.Cap.Obl@X5 ACCRA-IICASE ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@ DenominalAdjsC ; !^C^

 LEXICON PIERA !Bisyll. a-Proper Names without Gradation; a/i-Illative
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill@U.Cap.Obl@:j@U.Cap.Obl@ K ;
 ACCRA-DC ;
 @U.Cap.Obl@ ACCRA-OBL ;
 +N+Prop+š+Dimin@U.Cap.Obl@:ž@U.Cap.Obl@ PLACE-DIM-DECL ;

 @U.Cap.Obl@ GUOLBBA-OBL ;

LEXICON GUOLBBA-OBL 
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom:X4 K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:X4n K ;
 +N+Prop:X8 MALES ;		!^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:X2a K ; ! MALLAS- but for Prop
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:X2 K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:X2a R ; !^C^ compound also for these
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:X2 R ;  !^C^ compound also for these
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:X2a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:X2 K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:X2at K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:X2ij K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:X2is K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:X2ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:X2ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:X2ijd R ;	!^C^
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:X2ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:X2ijdda K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:X2ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:X2ijgujn K ;

 DenominalAdjsC ; !^C^

LEXICON ACCRA-DC
 @U.Cap.Obl@ ACCRA-NE ;
 @U.Cap.Opt@ ACCRA-ADJ ;
 
LEXICON ACCRA-NE
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;  ! To each Nom sg entry there is added an Attr tag
 +N+Prop+Sg+Attr: K ; ! it shall be used in cases like Konrad Nielsenii
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: R ;  !^C^
 +N+Prop+Ess:n K ;
 
LEXICON ACCRA-ADJ
 +N+Prop+laš:lažž DEARVVASLAS ;

LEXICON ACCRA-I
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:j K ;

LEXICON ACCRA-OBL
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:# R ; ! for placenames  !^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:s K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:jn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:t K ;

LEXICON ACCRA-IICASE
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:jde K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:jn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:jgujn K ;

! Vowel-final names where the final vowel carries
! primary or secondary stress. Monosyllables and
! Scandinavian stressed compounds in -V belong here.

LEXICON NYSTØ-fem
 NYSTØ ;
LEXICON NYSTØ-sur
 NYSTØ ;
LEXICON NYSTØ-plc ! Place names
 NYSTØ ;

LEXICON NYSTØ ! Vowel-final, heavy syll
 @U.Cap.Obl@ NYSTØ-OBL ;
 @U.Cap.Opt@ NYSTØ-DC ; !^C^

LEXICON NYSTØ-OBL 
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;	
 +N+Prop+Sg+Attr: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: R ;			!^C^
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:%:s K ; ! Nystø:s
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen#:a# R ; ! for placenames !^C^
 NYOBL ;
 :%: NYOBL ; ! to NYOBL, optional delimiter marks. sub?
 :%- NYOBL ;  
 :'1 NYOBL ; 

LEXICON NYSTØ-DC						!^C^
 +N+Prop+laš:lažž DEARVVASLAS ;		!^C^


LEXICON NYOBL
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:aj K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:as K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:an K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:ajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:ajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:ajde K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:ajgujn K ;

!checking for i- and a-base suffixes.

LEXICON PLACE-DIM
+N+Prop+š+Dimin: PLACE-DIM-DECL ;


LEXICON PLACE-DIM-DECL
 @U.Cap.Obl@ PLACE-DIM-OBL ;
! @U.Cap.Opt@ PLACE-DIM-DC ; !^C^

LEXICON PLACE-DIM-OBL
 +Sg+Nom: K ;
 +Sg+Nom:X7 R ;	!^C^
 +Ess:in K ;
 +Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +Sg+Gen: K ;
 +Sg+Gen:a R ; !^C^ compound also for these
 +Sg+Gen: R ;  !^C^ compound also for these
 +Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +Sg+Acc: K ;
 +Pl+Nom:at K ;
 :i PLACE-DIM-i ;

LEXICON PLACE-DIM-i
 +Sg+Ill:j K ;
 +Sg+Loc:s K ;
 +Sg+Com:jn K ;
 +Pl+Gen:jd K ;
 +Pl+Gen:jd R ;	!^C^
 +Pl+Acc:jd K ;
 +Pl+Ill:jdda K ;
 +Pl+Loc:jn K ;
 +Pl+Com:jgujn K ;

LEXICON PLACE-DIMV !DIMINV for propernouns
 +Sg+Nom: K ;
 +Sg+Nom: R ;                   !^C^ !Test this
 +Sg+Acc:aX4 K ; 
 +Sg+Gen:aX4 K ;
 +Sg+Gen:aX4 R ;		!^C^
 +Sg+Ill:aX3j K ;
 +Sg+Loc:aX4s K ;
 +Sg+Com:aX5jn K ;
 +Pl+Nom:aX4t K ;
 +Pl+Gen:aX5jd K ;
 +Pl+Acc:aX5jd K ;
 +Pl+Ill:aX5jde K ;
 +Pl+Loc:aX5jn K ;
 +Pl+Com:aX5jgujn K ;
 +Ess:an K ;

LEXICON C-FI-NEN-sur
! For Finnish surnames. Itkonen.
C-FI-NEN ;

LEXICON C-FI-NEN-plc
! For Finnish placenames with ending -nen. Kaustinen.
C-FI-NEN ;

LEXICON C-FI-NEN-surplc
! For Finnish names with ending -nen that are used both surnames and placenames. Huittinen.
C-FI-NEN ;

! Finnish Itkonen, lexicon for Finnish nen-names
LEXICON C-FI-NEN ! Finnish
 :nen3 LONDON ; ! In Norway, they are declined as CNAME
               ! with ordinary genitive Itkonena
 :s FI-S ;     ! In Finland, they are declined with
               ! Itkosa as the oblique stem.

! Finnish Itkosa
LEXICON FI-S
 @U.Cap.Obl@ FI-S-OBL ;
 @U.Cap.Opt@ FI-S-DC ; !^C^

LEXICON FI-S-OBL
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:# R ; ! For names !^C^

 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:ij K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:is K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:in K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:ijdda K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:ijgujn K ;

LEXICON FI-S-DC						!^C^
 +N+Prop+laš:lažž DEARVVASLAS ;		!^C^
